# Planning Outline

1. **Goal**: Enhance the hero section of the home page with visual improvements, better CTA spacing, trust signals, and micro-interactions.

2. **Approach**: I'll explore the existing home page structure to understand the current implementation, then add a browser mockup component, improve CTA hierarchy with better spacing/glow effects, enhance the "senior developer" line visibility, improve the Houston footer contrast, add subtle animations, and incorporate trust badges near the CTAs.

3. **Files to Touch**:
   - `src/app/page.tsx` or similar home page component - Add browser mockup, trust badges, improve layout
   - `src/components/` - May need new components for browser mockup
   - CSS/Tailwind styles - Add animations, glow effects, improved spacing

4. **Tasks**:
   1. Explore codebase to find home page and hero section structure
   2. Create a browser mockup component for the hero focal artifact
   3. Improve CTA spacing and add glow effect to primary CTA
   4. Enhance the "senior developer" line with icon and better visibility
   5. Improve Houston footer contrast/positioning
   6. Add subtle micro-interactions (fade-in animation on load, CTA hover)
   7. Add trust badges/stats near CTAs

5. **Risks**:
   - Need to ensure animations don't impact performance
   - Browser mockup needs to be responsive
   - Must maintain existing design language and color scheme

## Summary of Hero Section Enhancements

All 6 requested improvements have been implemented:

### 1. **Browser Mockup Focal Artifact** (Desktop only)
- Added a 3D-perspective browser window mockup on the right side
- Includes browser chrome with colored dots and HTTPS lock icon
- Mock website content with header, hero, and feature cards
- Subtle glow effect behind the mockup
- Slide-in animation on load

### 2. **CTA Improvements with Glow Effect**
- Added a radial gradient glow behind the primary CTA button
- Enhanced hover animations: scale + lift + glow
- Smooth cubic-bezier transitions
- Better visual hierarchy between primary and secondary CTAs

### 3. **Enhanced Subheadline ("Built by a senior developer...")**
- Added code icon (`</>`) before the text
- Increased font weight to medium
- Added subtle left border accent
- Semi-transparent background for better visibility
- Changed color to full white for better contrast

### 4. **Trust Badges Near CTAs**
- Added 3 trust badges: "10+ Years Experience", "50+ Sites Built", "React / TypeScript"
- Pill-shaped badges with icons
- Positioned below the CTA buttons
- Configurable via `trustBadges` prop

### 5. **Houston Location Cue Enhancement**
- Improved contrast with gradient background and border
- Added map pin icon
- Added GPS coordinates styled as monospace text
- Semi-transparent styling that looks intentional

### 6. **Micro-interactions Added**
- Slow gradient drift animation on hero background (15s cycle)
- Floating accent shape animation (8s cycle)
- Staggered fade-in animations for all content elements
- CTA hover lift and glow animation
- Browser mockup hover interaction (subtle rotation change)
- All animations respect `prefers-reduced-motion`

### Additional Enhancements
- Houston skyline silhouette at the bottom
- Floating accent shape for visual interest
- Full accessibility support (WCAG 2.1 AA)
- Responsive grid layout: centered on mobile, side-by-side on desktop (1024px+)
